          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

This vulnerability is similar to 



<span class="line"><!---->This vulnerability is similar to <!----></span>





issue 1320592



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1320592" title="Security: Heap-use-after-free in sharing_hub::SharingHubBubbleController::OnBubbleClosed"><!---->issue 1320592<!----></a>





, 



<span class="line"><!---->, <!----></span>





1336145



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1336145" title="Security: heap-use-after-free ash/system/tray/tray_bubble_view.cc (chromeOS)"><!---->1336145<!----></a>





.The bubble is closed via Close(), which is asynchronous.CookieControlsBubbleView can run after CookieControlsController object free.Then cause UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->.The bubble is closed via Close(), which is asynchronous.CookieControlsBubbleView can run after CookieControlsController object free.Then cause UAF.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->    content_settings::CookieControlsController* controller)<!----></span>

This PoC was very sparse on details. I think it is a legitimate bug but it took a lot of discussion to establish that.



<span class="line"><!---->This PoC was very sparse on details. I think it is a legitimate bug but it took a lot of discussion to establish that.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The controller is owned by the icon view, which has a lifetime that matches that of the browser window: 



<span class="line"><!---->The controller is owned by the icon view, which has a lifetime that matches that of the browser window: <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ui/views/location_bar/cookie_controls_icon_view.cc;l=109;drc=843911a994428b40537550f48b52d0d58cf08dd3



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ui/views/location_bar/cookie_controls_icon_view.cc;l=109;drc=843911a994428b40537550f48b52d0d58cf08dd3"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ui/views/location_bar/cookie_controls_icon_view.cc;l=109;drc=843911a994428b40537550f48b52d0d58cf08dd3<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





The bubble view is a self-owned widget, so it's lifetime is decoupled. ellyjones@ pointed out several ways that could close it, but noted in the case of something like the browser window closing, there's no guarantee about whether the bubble view or the icon view would be destroyed first.



<span class="line"><!---->The bubble view is a self-owned widget, so it's lifetime is decoupled. ellyjones@ pointed out several ways that could close it, but noted in the case of something like the browser window closing, there's no guarantee about whether the bubble view or the icon view would be destroyed first.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Since this is a browser-process UaF but is unlikely to be exploitable due to the user interactions required, I am going to mark this as medium.



<span class="line"><!---->Since this is a browser-process UaF but is unlikely to be exploitable due to the user interactions required, I am going to mark this as medium.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





(I am not sure if Mac uses views for this code, so I've not tagged Mac for now.)



<span class="line"><!---->(I am not sure if Mac uses views for this code, so I've not tagged Mac for now.)<!----></span>

CookieControls: Avoid potential UAF by adding WeakPtr



<span class="line"><!---->CookieControls: Avoid potential UAF by adding WeakPtr<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





CookieControlsBubbleView might access an invalid controller_ pointer



<span class="line"><!---->CookieControlsBubbleView might access an invalid controller_ pointer<!----></span>



<br>





if the icon is destroyed before the bubble. Use a WeakPtr to ensure



<span class="line"><!---->if the icon is destroyed before the bubble. Use a WeakPtr to ensure<!----></span>



<br>





that the pointer is still valid before accessing it.



<span class="line"><!---->that the pointer is still valid before accessing it.<!----></span>

[M102-LTS] CookieControls: Avoid potential UAF by adding WeakPtr



<span class="line"><!---->[M102-LTS] CookieControls: Avoid potential UAF by adding WeakPtr<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





CookieControlsBubbleView might access an invalid controller_ pointer



<span class="line"><!---->CookieControlsBubbleView might access an invalid controller_ pointer<!----></span>



<br>





if the icon is destroyed before the bubble. Use a WeakPtr to ensure



<span class="line"><!---->if the icon is destroyed before the bubble. Use a WeakPtr to ensure<!----></span>



<br>





that the pointer is still valid before accessing it.



<span class="line"><!---->that the pointer is still valid before accessing it.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





(cherry picked from commit 



<span class="line"><!---->(cherry picked from commit <!----></span>

[M96-LTS] CookieControls: Avoid potential UAF by adding WeakPtr



<span class="line"><!---->[M96-LTS] CookieControls: Avoid potential UAF by adding WeakPtr<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





M96 merge issues:



<span class="line"><!---->M96 merge issues:<!----></span>



<br>





  cookie_controls_bubble_view.h:



<span class="line"><!---->  cookie_controls_bubble_view.h:<!----></span>



<br>





    - include conflicts



<span class="line"><!---->    - include conflicts<!----></span>



<br>





    - conflicting data types for controller_



<span class="line"><!---->    - conflicting data types for controller_<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





CookieControlsBubbleView might access an invalid controller_ pointer



<span class="line"><!---->CookieControlsBubbleView might access an invalid controller_ pointer<!----></span>



<br>





if the icon is destroyed before the bubble. Use a WeakPtr to ensure



<span class="line"><!---->if the icon is destroyed before the bubble. Use a WeakPtr to ensure<!----></span>



<br>





that the pointer is still valid before accessing it.



<span class="line"><!---->that the pointer is still valid before accessing it.<!----></span>

          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
